 The defenders 



This year, in collaboration with Global Witness, the Guardian will attempt to record all of the deaths of people who are killed while defending their land, forests, rivers or wildlife

The toll: 20  Recording the deaths of environmental defenders around the world 



This year, in collaboration with Global Witness, the Guardian aims to record the deaths of all people killed while protecting land or natural resources. At the current rate, about four defenders will die this week somewhere on the planet

 From the agencies 
 Photo highlights of the day 
























Art Shay  Acclaimed photographer 


Shay, who has died aged 96, photographed celebrities, politicians and ordinary Americans during a career that spanned 70 years. His work for publications including Time, Life and Sports Illustrated made him one of the most respected photojournalists of his generation







 
Gallery






Acclaimed photographer

 




















Digital art and a lofty greenhouse  Thursday's top photos 


The Guardians picture editors bring you photo highlights from around the world







 
Gallery






Thursday's top photos

 
























Motor Mouths  A portrait of the UK car industry 



Motor Mouths, by the photographer and digital artist Richard Jones, offers an audiovisual insight into Britains automotive landscape





A portrait of the UK car industry

 




















Ice breakers  Finland's Unesco jetties 


Photographer Olivier Morin has produced a series of aerial images of jetties on the frozen Gulf of Bothnia around the Unesco-protected islands of the Merenkurkku archipelago in western Finland







 
Gallery






Finland's Unesco jetties

 




















Amazing grace  45 years of Cloud Gate Dance Theatre 


A Taiwanese company with a national day  21 August  and a street named after it, Cloud Gate Dance Theatre combine dance, martial arts, meditation and calligraphy in beautiful visual spectaculars







 
Gallery






45 years of Cloud Gate Dance Theatre

 




















Protests in Paris, May 1968  Photographs then and now 



As Paris exploded in mass protests, words scrawled on the walls of the Sorbonne summed up the revolutionary zeal: Run free, comrade, weve left the old world behind! Fifty years on, May 1968 remains a watershed moment. Photographer Alicia Canter revisits the key locations





Photographs then and now
